Sarah: Okay.

[They reach the snowy cabin on Mt. Thielsen's south side.]

Sarah: Was that here when you came over the pass?

Deacon: Yeah, but the soldiers stationed there were havin', uh — bear problems
        —

Sarah: Bear problems?

[Nearby is a new addition: a small manned checkpoint.]

Militia Soldier: Hey — hey! Shut it off! You're gonna have to turn around,
                 buddy. We got orders to keep anyone from —

Sarah: To keep anyone from what, Corporal?

Soldier: I'm sorry¹ ma'am. I didn't see it was you. It's — it's the Colonel,
         ma'am, he's given us orders to keep an eye out for anyone going AWOL —

Sarah: Are you accusing me of going AWOL?
Soldier: No¹ ma'am.
Sarah: Then get out of my way.

[Deacon turns the engine back on.]

Sarah: Corporal, what are you still doing there? Get the hell out of my way.
Soldier: Yes¹ ma'am. I'm sorry, ma'am.
Sarah: Jesus.
Soldier: I'll have to report this —
Sarah: Yeah, you do that.

[They ride through the checkpoint.]

Deacon: Well¹ that sounds serious.
Sarah: What do you mean?

Deacon: Well¹ he said he's gonna report you. I mean — how's Matt gonna take
        that?

Sarah: The Colonel will tell him to mind his own fucking business and to never
       question an officer. Oh my God.

Deacon: What's wrong?

Sarah: Nothing — it's just — I — I mean the view up here — it — it's
       incredible.

Deacon: Uh, yeah — I guess I — just don't see it anymore — pay attention to it,

Sarah: How can you not? It's — it's breathtaking —
Deacon: Yeah — the world wakes up, grateful for another dawn —

Sarah: Hey, if you spent all day staring into a microscope, you might

Deacon: Oh, I appreciate it — you know? Bein' around when the morning comes up

Sarah: I gotta be honest — you know, there were times when I didn't believe
       that — about, you know — hoping to see another day.

Deacon: Yeah, I know the feeling.
Sarah: What kept you going? I mean — back then?

Deacon: Um — I — I don't know. Just, uh — too Goddamn stubborn to give up, I
        think.

Sarah: I don't believe you.

Deacon: I did give up — Sarah. I did. And then, I don't know — Boozer's arm
        got fucked up — and I had to — I — I mean, I wasn't gonna let him die,

Sarah: Yeah, right.

Deacon: No, seriously — but, uh — then I remembered you still had my Mongrel's

        up — get it back. But you know how that turned out.

Sarah: Shit.
Deacon: Exactly.
Sarah: Things are gonna get better. You know that, right?
Deacon: Yeah —
Sarah: Yeah. We can win this thing, Deacon. We can.
Deacon: Are you tryin' to convince me? Or you?

Sarah: We must be getting close, right?

Deacon: Yeah. We're coming up on the Thielsen tunnel. I'm gonna need your help

[Sarah's eyes are drawn to mutilated corpses hanging from a branch.]

Sarah: My God — what the hell is that?
Deacon: That is a sigil. It's a warning sign from the Rippers.

Sarah: Sounds horrible.

Deacon: I've seen worse, but — yeah.

[Through the tunnel, they near the Cloverdale facility.]

Sarah: Hey, this looks familiar —
Deacon: Yeah, yeah — it's right up here.

114) I KNEW THESE PEOPLE                                                 [M114]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[The pair reaches the front gate.]

       but I never saw it.

        they do that?

Sarah: I don't know, Deacon. I dunno, I wasn't here.

[They walk closer to the main building. Sarah uses the scanning terminal.]

Sarah: Sarah Irene Whitaker. ID 2007659. Shit. This one's not working. Come
       on — there's another one over here.

Deacon: So, okay — so why is — um — what'd you call it? AIRI? Why is AIRI
        workin' at the front gate and not the front door?

[The two to the facility's north side to try another terminal.]

Sarah: Goddammit. I — I don't understand why these aren't working.
Deacon: Hey¹ Sarah — you know how you said no one could get in here?
Sarah: Yeah — why?

[He nods to a surveillance cam nearby.]

Deacon: Maybe they're already here.

Sarah: Motherfucker. My God, you're right. They've locked me out. Hey! Hey,
       let us in! We're not here to hurt you. And we're not here to stay! Oh¹

Sarah: Yeah. Yeah, I got an idea. Come on. There's a fire escape in the back

Deacon: But why won't they have that locked out too?

Sarah: We don't know that "they've" locked out anything — I mean, it's probably

[They walk to the facility's western side.]

Sarah: Here, this is it — I just have to figure out how to get up there —
Deacon: Hold on, hold on. Uh — I can shoot the latch —

[He snipes the latch holding the fire escape ladder in place.]

Sarah: Good shot — you done that before?
Deacon: Yeah, once or twice.

115) EXPECT THE WORST                                                    [M115]

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Deacon: Ah — fuckin' — Jesus Christ — Uh, hey¹ Captain — uh — pissed all over
        my bike —

Kouri: Uh — the Colonel doesn't allow for pets on the island, I'm afraid.
Deacon: Uh — Lieutenant needed a live test subject.
Kouri: Ah, you two seem to be getting along well. You and Lieutenant Whitaker.
Deacon: Just — doin' my job, sir.

Kouri: Yeah¹ well, keep it professional, Corporal. The Colonel doesn't allow
       for fraternization between enlisted men and officers.

Deacon: Oh, no, no — can't have any of that, sir.
Kouri: Right. Carry on.
Deacon: Yessir.

[Kouri leaves.]

Deacon: Okay, uh —

[He takes the Newt back to Sarah's tent, just as it starts coming around.]

Deacon: Come on, help me —
Sarah: Hold on, hold on —
Deacon: So much for your tranquilizer —

Sarah: Yeah, well¹ their biology is kinda fucked right now,¹ what do you want
       me to do? I can't get the right dosage. Here, hold on, hold that —

Deacon: Got it.

[The Newt is now hooked up to Sarah's IV bag.]

Sarah: Alright. This is it. This is what I've been working on.
Deacon: How long?
Sarah: Hold on, just a few seconds. Hold 'em — what?

[The struggling newt relaxes as it suddenly dies, blood leaking everywhere.]

Deacon: Oh shit. Holy shit. Goddamn. Well, I don't know what you put in that,
        but that shit went down fast.

Sarah: Oh — Goddammit!

Deacon: Wait, you — you're — you're not makin' a bio-weapon. You're — Oh my
        God, are you — are you — are you trying to cure it?

Sarah: I thought, that once I got the original cell line from Cloverdale — That
       I could create antibodies from the virus, and I could reverse¹ engineer
       it —

Deacon: Jesus.

Sarah: And now all of that work, everything that I have worked on is for
       nothing. I can't save them. Nothing's gonna be able to change them back.

Deacon: So get up. Dust yourself off. Try again.

Sarah: Were you not seeing what just happened? Every cell in that kid's body
       just exploded —

Deacon: That's exactly why you can't quit.
Sarah: What?

Deacon: Because you called it a "kid." Do you have any idea how many of these
        things that I've killed? And it never once occured to me, you know
        what? That used to be someone's kid. You know I met this girl once,
        and she used to talk about the Freakers the same way you do. She used
        to call them "sick people." I thought that was crazy — But she looks
        at them the same way that you do.

Sarah: So you think I'm crazy —

Deacon: No. No. I think you're the first sane person I've seen in two years.
        You know I still remember the night that I lost you, but — I'm starting
        to realize, it wasn't the night that I left you on that chopper. It was
        the next night. Me and Boozer, we rode into that refugee camp, that you
        were supposed to be waiting at, right? Except there's Freakers
        everywhere, the choppers are on fire, there's people screaming. So many
        people. And so we fought. And we won. And what do we get? Bodies.
        Bodies everywhere. And I checked every corpse, every face. There musta
        been a thousand of them — maybe more. I checked every single one. That
        was the night that I lost you. And, Boozer — Boozer¹ you know, he —
        he just — he was just trying — To keep me together for the next two
        years, but I didn't a shit about any of it. And then I see this NERO —
        chopper flying around in the sky — And I started to feel something,¹
        I'm thinking, you know what? Fuck you. Fuck you. Because even if she
        is alive, you know what I'm gonna do? I'm gonna find her, we're gonna
        ride away, we're never gonna look back. Because I don't wanna be part
        of some Militia, I don't wanna fight in a war. And I don't wanna live
        in some camp.

Sarah: So why are you still here?

Deacon: Because of you. All of this. Seeing how hard you work, seeing how
        dedicated you are. Most people out there, they're just trying to
        survive and here you are — Trying to save the Goddamn world.

Sarah: Yeah¹ well, I'm not doing a very good job.

Deacon: So you get up. Dust yourself off. And you try again. We're going back
        to Cloverdale. They got better equipment. We're gonna dig into their
        research deeper.

Sarah: You would do that? You would help me?
Deacon: Yeah¹ I would. I would because you believe in this. Don't give up.

Sarah: We'll ride north — Yeah, we'll ride north, we'll — we'll tell them that
       we're going on a supply run.

Deacon: Yeah, but we're not coming back.
Sarah: No, we're gonna go AWOL. You know if they catch us, they will hang us.
Deacon: Then we hang together.

[Just then, a soldier enters.]

Soldier: Ma'am.
Sarah: Yeah —
Soldier: Deek? Colonel wants to see you.
Deacon: Be right there.

[The soldier leaves.]

Deacon: Pack up what you need. I'll be back.
Sarah: Thank you.
Deacon: Yes¹ ma'am.

120) YOU ALONE I HAVE SEEN                                               [M120]

[As he leaves the tent, Garret walks by.]

[Deek gets into the slaughter.]

Deacon: Going down — yeah —
Kouri: Light 'em up! I can see 'em from here!

[After more finesse...]

Kouri: St. John — it looks like you're down to about half of them — keep going!
Deacon: I'm on it — Come on¹ you sonsofbitches —

Kouri: We did it. You did it!

Deacon: Ever had a Horde breathin' down your neck? It really keeps the
        adrenaline flowin'.

Kouri: Maybe the Colonel's right. Maybe we can win this war.

Weaver: Hey. How'd it go?

Weaver: Oh shit. It didn't work?

Kouri: I'm sorry, Lieutenant — but you're out of a job. Hell yeah, it worked.

Weaver: Oh — yeah?!

Deacon: You should've been there, man. We really lit 'em up.

Weaver: Oh man!

Kouri: We're gonna celebrate tonight! The officer's mess.

        coming?

Deacon: Uh, you know what? Let me — I'm gonna catch up with ya. I gotta — I
        gotta take care of something first.

Weaver: Alright, you handle that.

[Deek goes to Sarah's tent and finds her things being moved.]

Garret: That's the last of it. Be careful not to break anything. Some of these

Garret: Corporal St. John.

Deacon: I'm sorry, sir.

Garret: It's alright¹ son. All essential personnel doing R&amp;D have been moved.

Deacon: Moved? Where? Uh — because I need to deliver these supplies that she
        asked for.

Garret: I understand. There's — been a — Walk with me, son. Please.

[He leads her into the Ark where Sarah is under guard in her new lab.]

Soldier: Ma'am, Colonel's orders.

Sarah: Matt, you can't do this. You can't keep me locked in here!

Garret: At ease, Captain. "And then the Lord said to Noah, enter the ark, you
        and your household — For you alone I have seen to be righteous before
        Me in this time."

Sarah: What — Matt, what are you talking about?

Garret: I'm sorry, Lieutenant.

[Garret leaves.]

Sarah: You can't — Colonel, wait!

Deacon: Hey!

Sarah: It's fine. It's fine.

Deacon: Ma'am, I got the, uh, supplies that you asked for.

Sarah: Come on in, follow me. I've been working on a new assignment. Poison
       this time. Listen. When you pick this, you have to do it carefully. If
       you don't, it could kill you.

Deacon: Understood — 

[He then says quietly, to avoid the nearby guard's ears:]

Deacon: I'm gonna get you outta here.

Sarah: Thank you.

Deacon: Yes¹ ma'am.

[Deek leaves Sarah and her guard.]

124) WHAT IT TAKES TO SURVIVE                                            [M124]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[Earlier, after learning Sarah was under guard, Deacon goes for a drive.]

Deacon: O'Brian? Come in, O'Brian —  I know you're on this channel.

O'Brian: Drifter? I didn't think I'd ever hear from you again, the radio's
         been dead —

Deacon: Yeah, I turned it off. Look, I need your help.
O'Brian: I'm listening —
Deacon: My wife — the woman you helped me track down —
O'Brian: I remember.
Deacon: Well, I found her, O'Brian. She's alive.
O'Brian: That's — incredible. The odds of her making it out —

Deacon: No, look — I don't have time — look. I found her, she's alive, but
        she's being held — by — uh — the Militia, the guys that you told me

O'Brian: I'm sorry.

Deacon: Okay, look — I don't need your Goddamn sympathy — I need your help.
        She's being held — in a place — I can't get to her. I need you to help
        me to break her out.

O'Brian: You know I can't do that — wait a second — Okay. But there's something
         you have to do for us first.

Deacon: You name it — I will do anything.
O'Brian: Keep your radio on this time. I'll be in touch.
Deacon: Okay, O'Brian — O'Brian! Oh, dammit.

[Later...]

O'Brian: Drifter — are you there?
Deacon: O'Brian — okay — where the hell have you been?
O'Brian: Meet me at the coordinates I've just transmitted. O'Brian out.
Deacon: O'Brian? O'Brian? Oh, Jesus, he's — dammit.

[Deek follows the coordinates to the snowy mountains.]

Deacon: So, uh, what do you want from me, O'Brian?
O'Brian: I'm glad she's alive, your wife.
Deacon: Okay, what — what do you want?

O'Brian: I told you the infected — the Freaks — are mutating. Some faster than

Deacon: Uh-huh.

O'Brian: We placed a tracking bracelet on one of them — So that we could track
         it, and stop it periodically, and draw blood samples, and — Check the
         progress of the virus.

Deacon: Okay, so why do you need me?
O'Brian: Well¹ it's wandered into Militia territory.
Deacon: Ahh — right.
O'Brian: We can't get close to it.
Deacon: Yeah. No fly¹ zone. Outposts with RPGs.
O'Brian: Exactly.

[He hands Deacon a rectangular satchel.]

Deacon: What's this?

O'Brian: Once you've tracked it down, I'm gonna need you to do something for
         me. This pack holds everything you need to do a field biopsy. We need
         blood and tissue samples. Can you handle that?

Deacon: Yeah, I can figure it out.
O'Brian: By the way. Nice uniform, Corporal. Suits you.
Deacon: Suck it.

[O'Brian leaves, but radios in soon after.]

O'Brian: The tracking signal is coming from somewhere around Mt. Scott. There's
         a cave. The subject you're tracking has a super elevated metabolism.
         We think it might be headed there. There's something else we'd like
         you to check — We did send a team in — on foot. They never came back.
         Just — let me know if you find 'em. We got people here looking for

Deacon: So, uh — what else can you tell me about this Freak you're trackin'?

O'Brian: We don't have all the answers. All we know is the infected are
         mutating. We're talking about leaping past millions of years of
         evolution. We think they're communicating with each other the way
         ants, and bees, and — and other —

Deacon: Y'know — to me, it sounds like a whole lotta mumbo jumbo.

O'Brian: Believe what you want. Once you see our test subject, you'll change
         your mind. O'Brian out.

[Deek travels to the Ice Wind Lava Cave near Mt. Scott.]

Deacon: O'Brian, I'm at the cave and I'm headin' in. You guys gonna be ready?
O'Brian: Yes. We're standing by.
Deacon: Oh Jesus.
O'Brian: What's wrong?

Deacon: Freaker shit — Freaker shit everywhere. Hey¹ O'Brian — uh — you got
        any idea what took out your men? Am I walking into a Horde here?

O'Brian: No idea. We never heard back from them. Remember, if you find them,
         we got people here who'd be grateful.

Deacon: Grateful, grateful, yeah¹ that changes everything. Yeah — I got it.
        Good. I'll take care of it. Out. O'Brian — how many men are in here?
        Uh, how many did — did you lose?

O'Brian: Four.
Deacon: Four men.
O'Brian: A researcher and three soldiers.
Deacon: Jesus, O'Brian. What am I doin' in here?

O'Brian: The researcher — Coop — is a personal friend of mine. You do this,
         and I'll do whatever I can to help you get your wife. O'Brian out.

[Deek heads inside.]

Deacon: O'Brian — so while I'm tracking down your pet Freak, give me some more
        mumbo jumbo. Uh — tell me about the virus. I mean, somethin' that I
        don't know.

O'Brian: For those exposed, the virus infection rate is close to 100%. In the
         first weeks, almost everyone under the age of twelve was killed.
         Something to do with how puberty, or the lack of it, affected the
         body's immune response. Everyone over the age of sixty, mostly, were
         also killed. Their bodies just couldn't handle the rapid genetic
         mutations on a cellular level. Everyone else who is exposed becomes
         transformed as the genes mutate. The thing is — the virus is mutating
         at an exponential rate.

Deacon: I know, you keep saying that. What does that mean?

O'Brian: It means that the infected subject — the Freaker you're tracking down
         — isn't like any you've seen before. We've tracked and identified over
         twelve mutations.

Deacon: Twelve.

O'Brian: Yeah. And that's just the beginning. You wouldn't believe some of the
         shit we've seen.

Deacon: Yeah, well — I probably would. St. John out.

[A short ways into the cave...]

Deacon: A flare. Shit, that's gotta be one of O'Brian's men. Uh — hey¹ you, up
        there! Can you hear me? O'Brian — I see one of your men.

O'Brian: Is he — alive?

Deacon: I don't know,¹ he's not answering. And, uh — he's on a ledge above me.
        I'll see if I can get up to him.

O'Brian: If you can, retrieve his ID badge.

Deacon: Yeah, yeah. I'll get right on that. St. John out. How the hell am I
        gonna get up there?

[He looks at some tracks.]

Deacon: Guys in yellow spacesuits — can't be too hard to find 'em if they're
        in here — NERO equipment — musta, well, come this way. Maybe this way —

[He tries to get up to the first-spotted soldier and succeeds.]

Deacon: Another flare — yeah, this has to be the way. O'Brian, I, uh — I
        reached your guy and, uh — yeah. He's dead. ID says G. Hernandez.

O'Brian: How did it happen?

Deacon: Well, I'm not a coroner, O'Brian. How the hell do I know? Somethin' —
        tore him apart. This Freak I'm trackin' — is there somethin' you
        haven't told me?

O'Brian: Not that I'm aware of. O'Brian out.

[He soon finds a second corpse and observes the scene.]

Deacon: What the hell was that? He went down fast. O'Brian, I found another one
        of your men. ID says his name was H.S. Patterson.

O'Brian: Okay. Thanks for letting me know.
Deacon: You didn't ask, O'Brian.
O'Brian: Didn't ask what?
Deacon: If he was alive or dead.

O'Brian: His radio's been dead for twelve hours. All their radios have been
         dead for twelve — hours. I don't need to ask. Thank you for doing
         this. O'Brian out.

[He keeps spelunking in almost pitch darkness.]

Deacon: How am I gonna get to him? Another flare — gotta be another one of
        O'Brian's men. Hello! Can you hear me? Move an arm or something, if you
        can hear me! Move an arm — nope. Just gotta find a way over there.

[Deek hops a guide railing to find another flare.]

Deacon: Down there maybe.

[He soon finds a third corpse.]

Deacon: What the hell hit you? You didn't even see it coming. O'Brian, I, uh —
        found another one. ID says his name was Robinson.

O'Brian: Okay. Thanks. I'll — let his family know.

Deacon: So you guys have, uh — families. Managed to get 'em all out while shit
        was going down?

O'Brian: I'm not gonna apologize for being — lucky — luckier than most. Yes,
         some of us got our families out. Not many, but — some.

Deacon: That's just — that's so great, O'Brian. Good for you.
O'Brian: We didn't ask for this.
Deacon: Yeah — neither did anyone else.

[Deek sets off to find Cooper.]

Deacon: There's the last one —

O'Brian: Cooper, are you there? Is anyone there? NERO Team Bravo, come in. This
         is Commander James O'Brian — respond — if you are receiving this
         transmission. Coop — answer me —

Deacon: A NERO radio — this way.

[He observes another blood trail.]

Deacon: Must be Cooper — what the hell were you doing down here, man?

[He climbs into a wide-open space with lots of bones and blood spatter.]

Deacon: Yeah — that doesn't look good. Oh, shit — what the hell happened?
        O'Brian, I found your last man. ID reads Cooper.

O'Brian: Copy that.

[Suddenly, Cooper's body spasms to life.]

Cooper: Oh no —
Deacon: Oh Jesus.
Cooper: No, no!

Deacon: Hold on, he's still alive. Hold on — hey, Cooper, Cooper — Hey, hey,
        hey, hey, hey — right here, right here! We're gonna get you outta here,
        alright¹ pal?

O'Brian: Cooper? Cooper, come in.
Cooper: Sorry — shit — went south. Team's down.
Deacon: C'mon.

[He's in too much pain to help up.]

Deacon: Oh, Jesus.
O'Brian: What's going on? Deacon? Cooper?
Deacon: His legs are broken.
O'Brian: Hold on, stay with him. I'm sending in another team.

Cooper: No! No, no — My suit's compromised — I'm not gonna make it. Let me
        talk to Jean.

Deacon: Hey —
O'Brian: Get Jenn in here, now!
Deacon: Cooper, what the hell did this to you? What happened?
Cooper: It moved so fast. Didn't — didn't see — see it coming —
Deacon: Are you telling me that a Freak did all of this?
Cooper: Reacher — The Reacher —
Jenn: Cooper? Cooper, are you there?!
Cooper: Jenn?
Jenn: Uh-huh — I'm here — I can hear you —
Cooper: I can't believe it — I thought I'd never hear your voice — again —

Jenn: Coop — listen to me. We're gonna get you out of there — do you hear me?
      Coop — Coop —

Cooper: Jenn, I'm so glad I got to hear your — voice —
Jenn: Coop? Coop?! No — no!

[Cooper succumbs to his injuries.]

O'Brian: Jenn, come on —
Jenn: Let go of me! Let — Get your hands off me!
O'Brian: Get her outta here!
Deacon: He's gone.
O'Brian: Copy that. O'Brian out.
Deacon: Reacher —

[He hears a guttural growling nearby and spots something moving quickly.]

Deacon: Oh, what the hell? So what the hell am I dealing with here, O'Brian?
        Talk to me.

O'Brian: The guys at the lab nicknamed it the Reacher.
Deacon: The Reacher? What, it's got long arms? Claws? What?
O'Brian: No, it's just — fast. We've clocked it moving forty miles an hour.
Deacon: Forty — Jesus.
O'Brian: And yeah, it's strong. Maybe you should abort —
Deacon: No, no, no, to hell with that. I'm not aborting anything.
O'Brian: This isn't your fight.
Deacon: It is now. St. John out.

[After a lot of hide-and-seek, Deacon guns down the Reacher.]

O'Brian: The Reacher should have a tracking device — take it! Take it! We can
         use it to guide you out.

Deacon: What? How, how O'Brian.¹

O'Brian: We have infrared — we can track the Horde's movements. Take it.

[He walks over to the new corpse to do a biopsy.]

Deacon: Oh Jesus — I hope this was worth it, O'Brian. O'Brian. I got your
        samples.

O'Brian: St. John, get out of there!
Deacon: What?
O'Brian: Get out of there — now! There's a Horde coming —
Deacon: You gotta be kidding me —
O'Brian: Shit, they're gettin' close —
Deacon: Yeah — it's time to finish these guys off —

[Deek leaves after killing the bite-sized horde.]

Deacon: Jesus, O'Brian.
O'Brian: You made it out.
Deacon: Yeah, I made it out, no thanks to you.
O'Brian: Transmitting coordinates. O'Brian out.

[They rendezvous far away from the cave.]

Deacon: O'Brian. Four men died for this shit. Hope it was worth it.

O'Brian: Jesus, listen to you. Those were my men! I don't need you or anyone
         else telling me how —

Deacon: You know, you fly around in your helo, well above the shit. And you
        crawl back into, what? Cozy underground bunker, whatever the fuck. You
        have no idea what it's like out here —

O'Brian: I don't have to listen to this shit —

Deacon: What it takes to survive. Oh, you know those men, Cooper — the others,
        they had no idea what they were walking into, but you did. Didn't you?
        Huh? Didn't you!¹

O'Brian: Radio me when you and your old lady are ready to be lifted out. Maybe
         this time, you'll get on the chopper with her.

[O'Brian leaves in a huff and flies out.]

125) THE ANARCHIST SPY                                                   [M125]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After learning Sarah was put under guard in the ark, Garret radios in.]

Garret: Corporal St. John. This is Colonel Garret. Report.
Deacon: Yes¹ sir.

Garret: Corporal. Good. Yes — another traitor was discovered in our midst — a
        spy, working for the Anarchists.

Deacon: Anarchists — again —

Garret: Yes — you remember. He escaped before he could be — apprehended. He was
        chased north, but our patrol lost him. I've marked the position he was
        last seen on your map. We need him alive, Corporal. We need to find out
        what he was doing here — how much he knows — what his group wants.

Deacon: Yes¹ sir. I'll do my best.
Garret: As do we all — as do we all. Dismissed.

[Deek goes to the last-known location.]

Garret: A word of caution — Captain Kouri tells me he was one of our best
        riders — if you let him get away — you won't be able to catch him.

Deacon: Ah, we'll just see about that. St. John out.

[Deacon searches a corpse in a snowy cabin. The rider's flushed just then.]

Deacon: Colonel, I've spotted him. Oh, come on — you're not gonna make this
        easy on me, are ya?

[After a short chase, Deacon unseats the Anarchist and blows up his bike.]

Deacon: Got him! Oh, Goddamn —

[Soon, the villain is hogtied helplessly.]

Deacon: How you doin'¹ buddy, huh? Looks like you're having a — chaotic — day,
        yeah? Just the way you like it?

Marauder: You won't take me alive —

Deacon: Well, I think I already did — don't matter much to me, one way or the
        other. Goddamn Anarchists. Colonel, I've got him. Transmitting the
        coordinates now.

Garret: Good work, Corporal.

[Deek leaves the pleading Anarchist on the snowy highway and leaves. Later...]

Deacon: Colonel, reporting in. Did the, uh — patrol get the prisoner?
Garret: Corporal. I'm afraid not. When we went to retrieve him — he was dead.
Deacon: Wha — dead?
Garret: Poison. He killed himself. We're not sure how.
Deacon: I'm sorry. Sir.
Garret: Don't be. Whatever knowledge he had about us — died with him.
Deacon: Yes¹ sir. St. John out.

126) SHADOW OF DEATH                                                     [M126]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After finishing up missions for Sarah, Garret, Weaver and O'Brian, Deacon
 returns back to Wizard Island. He sees the colonel giving another speech.]

Garret: I have had a — revelation. Last night, a new group of recruits joined
        our ranks and have already been sworn in. They have travelled far,
        from the east, west, south, and north. Their coming to this place, at
        this time, is no accident. They bring word of more camps, like the one
        to the south, which we have purged,¹ camps filled with degenerates,
        thieves, drug addicts, and murderers. We are threatened! All of us!
        Every day we live in the shadow of death. But that shadow is not cast
        by rabid Freaks that surround us. They are part of God's plan. They
        are part of God's punishment. No! No, it is not the Freaks who threaten
        to destroy us. It is our fellow man. Like Noah before us, we have built
        an ark, to save mankind. To save all the knowledge¹ so that when the
        flood waters recede, we may rebuild. But in this age, here at the end
        of the world — God is not sending the oceans from their beds to rise up
        and sweep away the damned. There will be no baptism of water. No. In
        this last age, we are the flood. We are sent forth, to baptize the
        world — with fire! Today, we begin a Holy War against all those who
        have brought down the wrath of God. We will move north! Seek out the
        depraved and cleanse them — from the world. We will move south, find
        the enclaves of the degenerates and destroy them. We will head east —
        uncover the obscene and purge them. We will head west, cast light —

[Deacon walks away from the mad colonel and his bonfire-captivated crowd.]

Deacon: O'Brian. This is St. John, come in.
O'Brian: I'm here.

Deacon: Okay, I hope you're ready, because we're doin' this. We're doin' this
        right now.

O'Brian: Give me your coordinates.
Deacon: Done.
O'Brian: Wait — where are you?
Deacon: Center of Crater Lake — Wizard Island, the Militia camp.
O'Brian: You disabled the RPGs?
Deacon: Ah shit, not yet — I'll get right on that.
O'Brian: Radio me when you're ready. O'Brian out.

Deacon: Gotta get to the RPGs — Where would they be — oh, the towers — it's
        gotta be the towers.

[He goes near a tower and sees soldiers loafing about.]

Deacon: That's right — keep movin' —
Soldier: Hell, man. Did you hear the Colonel's speech?
Officer: But movin' against other camps? Jesus — that's harsh —
Soldier: Find me some grub while you're out.
Officer: Yeah, right.

[When no one's looking, Deacon tampers with the RPG.]

Deacon: Come on, you sonofabitch — That'll do it — Gotta get to Sarah — Sarah —
        Lieutenant Whitaker — come in.

[There's only static.]

Deacon: Dammit — hang on. I'm comin'.

[He visits her lab in the ark. She's conversing with her "bodyguard."]

Sarah: Can't you stand guard — or do whatever it is you're doing — out there?
Soldier: Colonel's orders. Gotta keep eyes on you at all times.
Sarah: Yeah, well, fuck the Colonel's orders.

Soldier: Hey. You watch your mouth. Things are changin' around here. And if you
         don't follow the order —

[Deacon sneaks up on him and KOs him with a sleeper hold.]

Deacon: Make sure we're clear.
Sarah: You're good, you're clear. What's the plan?
Deacon: Okay. I need you to pack your stuff. We're leavin'.
Sarah: How are we gonna get out of here? There are guards everywhere.
Deacon: Hey, do you trust me?

[He flips out his radio.]

Deacon: O'Brian?
O'Brian: I'm here.
Deacon: We're heading up to the cone — we got one shot at this.
O'Brian: Copy that. O'Brian out.
Sarah: Who's O'Brian? Where are we going?

Deacon: Look, I don't have time to explain. You got everything? We're not
        coming back.

Sarah: Yeah, I'm ready,¹ let's go.
Deacon: Alright, stay close, and if we see anyone —
Sarah: Hey —

[She suddenly kisses him.]

Sarah: In case you didn't read my note.

[They start their inner ascent.]

Sarah: Wait, so who's O'Brian? How's he getting us out of here?

Deacon: I told you — O'Brian is how I found you. He was the NERO soldier who
        was there that night — the night that I put you on that chopper —

Sarah: NERO?
Deacon: Oh, shit — Weaver —
Weaver: Look — come on, I need you guys to move these out of the way.

[They sneak into the nursery. Only Weaver knows they're there.]

Weaver: No, no, no. That one. The canister. Right. Private! Are you payin'
        attention? Eyes on your work, man. That canister. Right there.

[When the attendants are distracted, Weaver nods to the pair.]

Deacon: Okay — go, go!
Weaver: Up! I don't want to see that canister fall —

[They sneak past Weaver and his attendants.]

Sarah: Holy shit — he let us go. Weaver let us go. Oh shit — more guards.
Deacon: Okay, hold here.
Sarah: Hey, come on,¹ let's go around them.
Deacon: Okay —
Sarah: So O'Brian — the guy on the NERO chopper — he's coming here?

Deacon: Yeah — look, it's a long story. I'll tell ya all about it once we get
        clear —

Sarah: Wait, so they're still flying? I mean — God, Deacon, they must have
       resources, labs, equipment —

Deacon: Well¹ yeah, I — I'm pretty sure they do. Look — you can ask O'Brian
        when you see him —

Sarah: Another guard. Hold on, I'll distract 'em.
Deacon: Be careful —

[As Deacon hides, Sarah goes up to the sentry.]

Sarah: Soldier — what are you doing?

Officer: I — I'm sorry¹ ma'am — the — this area is off limits —

Sarah: How dare you talk back to an officer.¹ Do you know the penalty for
       disobeying an order? Do you know that we have hanged soldiers for less?
       You do know that, right? I was sent by the Colonel, soldier. He's asked
       me to check on you, specifically you. He mentioned you by name. Do you
       know what that means? Do you?

[Deacon puts him in a sleeper.]

Soldier: Hey — what —
Deacon: Nice.
Sarah: Another guard. I'll see if I can get them to move.
Deacon: Be careful —

[Sarah skips the distraction and sleepers the guard herself.]

Deacon: Well done.
Sarah: Come on — we're almost there. I can't wait to see Boozer again —

Deacon: You, uh — you want to go with me, to Lost Lake — I mean. I mean — I —
        I thought we were going to Cloverdale —

Sarah: No, we are. I mean — I just want to see him. He's like my big brother.
       I don't know, it's not like we have much family left these days — you
       know?

[Another sentry's nearby.]

Sarah: Wait — I'll distract 'em. Soldier — over here, please!
Soldier: Ma'am? This is restricted —

Sarah: Are you questioning me, soldier? Do you see this rank? Huh? Do you know
       that I can have you court-martialed for insubordination, disobeying
       orders, and generally being disrespectful to an officer? Do you know
       who I am? Do you know that I am an officer? That I work directly with
       Colonel Garret? That I have two PhDs in bio-medical science? Are you
       questioning me?

Soldier: Hey — what —

[Deacon puts him to sleep.]

Sarah: Good work.
Deacon: Yeah, you too.
Sarah: I can see daylight. Come on, we're almost out.
Deacon: Yeah, okay, this is it, we're at the cone.

[They finally exit the interior caves.]

Deacon: Okay. We made it.
Sarah: Where is it? Where is he? Where is O'Brian?
Deacon: He'll be here. He'll be here. We just, uh, need to —
Sarah: Oh shit!
Deacon: Oh no —

[Just then, Garret walks out of his tent on tour with some new recruits.]

Garret: Gentlemen¹ this is the top of the cone where you can see we get an
        amazing view here — Oh, Lieutenant! I've just been giving this group
        of new recruits a tour of the island. Oh, we're just about to go down

Sarah: Oh, well, Colonel —

Garret: Gentlemen, this is Lieutenant Whitaker. She heads up part of the

        enemies.

[Just then, Skizzo walks out of Garret's tent.]

Skizzo: Traitor!

[Skizzo lunges at Deacon.]

Sarah: What? Wait!
Garret: Wait — wait, no, stay back!

[O'Brian's chopper comes overhead, hovers a moment, and flies off. Deacon and
 Sarah are taken down to Garret's chambers in the ark.]

Sarah: Matt, I was just trying to tell you that were going on a supply run.
Skizzo: Don't listen to her! He's a murderer and a spy.
Sarah: Why would you listen to him over me? You know me Matt.

Skizzo: Do you remember the camp I told you about? Iron Mike, the leader of

Deacon: Oh, this is full of shit. I — I've never even met this motherfucker.
Skizzo: Colonel, you've gotta believe me!
Garret: Enough! Alright. I'm listening.
Skizzo: I am tellin' you. He is a spy.

Sarah: Matt¹ this guy's crazy,¹ you've never seen him before — He comes out of
       nowhere and you're gonna believe him?

Deacon: He's fuckin' lying. What's that camp you're saying I'm from?
        Lost what-the-fuck?

Skizzo: You think I'm lying? You think I'm lying? Is that it? I'm not lying.

Garret: Enough! Enough! That's my last warning. Now, we will get to the truth
        of this matter. Thou shalt not bear false witness against thy neighbor.

Kouri: I don't rightly recall, sir.
Garret: Tell me what you saw and don't lie to me, son. I'll know.
Skizzo: At Lost Lake Camp, he attacked a woman.
Deacon: What the fuck are you talk —
Garret: Corporal!

Skizzo: He wasn't wearin' a shirt. Sonofabitch has a tattoo, covering his back.

[Garret motions for soldiers to pick Deacon up.]

Deacon: I'm sorry¹ Colonel, this shit's just so crazy.

[They rip his shirt to reveal his tattooed back.]

Garret: Turn him.

[He sees the tattoo.]

Garret: You wear the image of Cerberus, the Hound of Hades. How fitting, that
        you were discovered ascending from the underworld. But you are not
        Hades, are you? Deacon St. John.

Deacon: He's lyin' to you. I never hurt anyone and the truth is —

Garret: You hide behind angelic names, and clothe yourself in lies. You are
        Judas!

Deacon: Truth is, he got kicked out of camp. Listen to me —

[He punches Deacon hard in the stomach.]

Garret: And what about you, Lieutenant? How convenient that you were with the
        Drifter when the NERO helicopter came by.

Sarah: Colonel, I do not know what you're talking about.

Garret: You were in a NERO camp that was overrun. How long have you been spying
        on us? How long?

Sarah: Matt, I promise, I haven't been —
Garret: More lies!

[He backhands her and points a revolver at her head.]

Garret: I expect this from Drifters. I expect men like him to betray me. But
        an officer?

Kouri: Colonel —

Deacon: It was me! It was me. Colonel, I lied. If you look in my pocket, you're
        gonna find a radio. Because I called them. I called them and I lied. I
        lied to the Lieutenant — I told her that, uh, I needed her to help me
        check a shipment, but — Truth is I just needed a hostage.

O'Brian: Deacon St. John? Drifter¹ are you there? This is NERO, this is
         O'Brian. Drifter?

Garret: I'm sorry, Corporal St. John is unavailable right now.
O'Brian: Wait. Who is this?

[Garret stomps on the radio.]

Garret: Sometimes, in the search for truth, the blood of innocents is spilled.
        I'm sorry, my dear.

[He puts his sidearm away.]

Garret: Release Private — Sarkozi, was it?
Skizzo: Yeah.

Garret: And Kouri, take this Drifter to lockup. Tomorrow, at oh-seven-hundred,
        he will stand trial, and he will hang. Lieutenant. Enough of this. We
        have work to do. Come.

[Garret leaves with Skizzo.]

Garret: Tell me more about this Lost Lake Camp.
Skizzo: Yes¹ sir. Anything you wanna know.
Garret: Lieutenant! Please.
Kouri: Come on. Get up.

[He feebly tries to get free, but Kouri coldcocks him.]

127) ASCENDING FROM THE UNDERWORLD                                       [M127]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[When he comes to, he's outside of town with Kouri and some other soldiers at
 a campfire. He's not restrained.]

Kouri: Good. I thought I heard you breathin'.
Deacon: Fuck you —
Kouri: That's what I want to hear. Means the shit hasn't broken you yet.

Kouri: Tat on your back — a dead dog chewing through its chains? Not something

[He holds up the Mongrel's ring.]

Kouri: My guess is, it's yours.

[He tosses it to Deacon.]

Deacon: Yeah, it's mine.

Deacon: Wait — wait a — wait a second, you're — you're — you're helping me?
        Well¹ that — that just means you're all gonna hang —

Kouri: We're not goin' back. The Colonel is batshit crazy. Holy war? Genocide?
       I mean, what the fuck is that?

Deacon: Yeah, well then, what's the plan? What are you going to do?

Kouri: We're going east. Yeah. Hopefully we can make it to Reno. You should

Deacon: Nope.
Kouri: Well, you can't go back. The Militia will shoot you on sight —

Deacon: No, I am not leaving without her, uh — and I gotta ride north, I gotta

Deacon: Yeah. We're gonna stop him.

        he was — he was only trying to — do the right thing.

Deacon: Almost — done —

[Finally, every Freaker lies still.]

Deacon: And that — my friend — is all of 'em — Jesus — Boozeman, you there?

Copeland: This is Radio Free Oregon. The Truth Shall Set You Free. Many of you
          probably don't remember the Cold War, but living through it was a
          special kind of hell. Every time you heard a plane flyin' overhead,
          you'd think for sure that this is it, that's the one coming to drop
          the big one on us. And we lived through the Red Scare. A man didn't
          know if his neighbor was an American who bled red, white, and blue,
          or a Communist, red to the bone. Made it hard to trust. My father —
          God rest him — taught me the only way to be safe in dark times was
          to go underground. Built my first bunker with him. But we couldn't
          build it out in the backyard, with the neighbors spyin'. Had to go
          out into the woods, a ways from the road, where no one would happen
          upon it. With a bunker, you knew that if the country went to hell in
          a handbasket, you could open that manhole cover, climb down the
          ladder, and you'd be safe — with your radio, and your hoard of food
          and ammo. Things haven't changed. Better to dig a bunker, than an
          early grave. This is Mark Copeland for Radio Free Oregon. Don't
          believe the lies.

Deacon: Yeah, Cope? How'd that work out for the poor bastards who owned the one
        that I just cleared out? Huh? Not so good, I'm guessing, since they
        were all dead long before I ever got there.

133) NOSE DOWN, THEY FEED YA                                             [M133]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[Deek rides out to the Squatter camp to save Manny. He sees a bike nearby.]

Manny: Shit.

Deacon: So the question isn't — why is it like this now,¹ the question is why

Manny: Guess I'll be stickin' to the camp from now on.

Manny: Yeah, yeah. Hey¹ Deek? I owe you, man. I'd be dead right now if it you

Deacon: Cope, I found him.

Copeland: Thank God and country. He's alive?

Deacon: He's a little banged up, but he'll live. I'm guessin' a few Drifters

Copeland: I hope he told 'em — we have all the damn guns we need. And we mean
          to keep 'em. Feds don't got no more to say about that, now do they?

Deacon: No, I guess they don't. Manny gets back, tell him to keep his nose
        down. St. John out.

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After taking care of lingering Militia concerns...]

Boozer: Alright¹ brother, you're killin' me. Where you getting the creosote?
Deacon: You just like driving that dump truck around.
Boozer: You're Goddamn right I do.

Deacon: Alright, um — I'm headin' to the Old Sawmill. They got a couple of
        storage tanks there that should have all the creosote we need.

Boozer: The Old Sawmill? Last I checked, there was a Horde there. Big Goddamn
        Horde.

Deacon: Yeah. I'm, uh — pretty sure I knew that.
Boozer: What, you still got a death wish? I mean, even after finding your old
        lady? Deek — we're gonna get her back —

Deacon: Boozeman — no, no — I don't — look, I can handle this. Just be ready.
        I'll radio when it's clear to bring your rig in. Deacon out.

[Soon after...]

Rikki: Deek?
Deacon: Yeah¹ Rikki.
Rikki: Boozer just told me you're heading for the Old Sawmill.
Deacon: Uh, yeah — and Boozer has a big mouth.

Rikki: He is head of security — he has to tell me. You remember when I took
       you to the sawmill, right? You remember me showing you the Horde that —
       lives there?

Deacon: Oh yeah — I remember.
Rikki: The really big Horde that lives, sleeps, and eats there?

Deacon: Uh, yeah, like I said — I remember. Uh¹ look, Rikki — when I was with
        the Militia — they, uh — we — we created a sorta souped¹ up Molotov —

Rikki: A souped¹ up Molotov —
Deacon: Yeah, yeah — it's — it's like napalm. Anyway, trust me — I got this —
Rikki: We need you, Deek — alive —

Deacon: Rikki — just — I'll be fine. You don't gotta worry about me no more —
        okay? I know what I'm doing. Rikki?

Rikki: Yeah¹ Deek —
Deacon: I'm, uh — just lightin' some candles.
Rikki: Okay.

Deacon: Yeah — and in — in this case, some big Goddamn Molotovs — but, you
        know, you get the idea —

Rikki: Yeah, okay.
Deacon: Deacon out.

[He arrives at the destination.]

Deacon: The Old Sawmill. This oughta be — easy, right? Just gotta make sure I
        have enough, uh — traps, ammo, Molotovs, and anything else I can
        carry —

[He riles the crowd.]

Deacon: Oh my God this is a lot of Freaks — Too many — too many! Crawl under
        here — go, go — Ah shit — more of 'em! C'mon — is that all you got?
        Is that all of 'em — oh yeah — oh Jesus —

[At long last, the Horde expires. Boozer arrives afterwards.]

Boozer: Holy shit, Deek. Looks like I missed all the fun.
Deacon: Yeah. Next time — I drive the truck. You fight the Freakers.
Boozer: Yeah, brother.
Deacon: Okay, just pull it over there.
Boozer: Alright, you got it.

[Soon, the creosote is loaded.]

Deacon: Alright, that's it. Head back to camp. I'll meet you there.
Boozer: Alright.
Deacon: And — uh — Boozeman. Drive carefully.
Boozer: Whaddya think? That I'm gonna blow myself up?

[Boozer heads out.]

Rikki: Hey¹ Deek — you there?
Deacon: Hey¹ Rikki — what's up?

Rikki: There's still some work I need to do on the truck — uh — I'll radio you
       when it's ready.

Deacon: Thank you, thank you — uh, I'm ready when you are.
Rikki: Deek, you sure you wanna do this?
Deacon: They're coming — Rikki — unless we take 'em out first.
Rikki: You're right. Okay. Rikki out.

135) YOU CAN'T DO THIS ALONE                                             [M135]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[Deek goes into Lost Lake following the successful Sawmill operation.]

Deacon: Looks like everything's set.

Boozer: Yeah. Rikki rigged this up for the steering wheel. We drive right up
        to the front door, jump — goodbye¹ Militia.

Deacon: Okay, well, you sure you wanna do this? I mean, it's a long way to
        drive with only one arm.

Boozer: Asshole.
Deacon: Look, Boozer, you and I both know this is probably a one-way trip.

Boozer: Yeah. Then I won't have to drive back. Fuck yeah, I want this. Oh, but
        there's just one thing —

[He gets a familiar clothing item from the cab.]

Boozer: Only a coupla bikers — would pull a dumbass stunt like this.
Deacon: Just us.
Boozer: Yep.

[Deek puts his Mongrels cut back on. They stand awkwardly for a few seconds.]

Deacon: We're gonna do this? Or what?
Boozer: Goddamn straight.

[Soon, another bike pulls out of Lost Lake.]

Boozer: Looks like Rikki's comin' after all.
Rikki: What's up, Deek? Nice jacket. Looks good on you.

Deacon: Rikki — Addy — I appreciate it, but — Boozer and I, we — we got — we
        gotta take of some stuff —

[Lost Lake practically empties as riders stream out to join the fight.]

Rikki: Word gets around. Your speech touched more people than you thought,
       Deek. I told you. You can't do this alone.

Deacon: This — this is crazy —
Rikki: Oh, don't worry. They're not doing it for you. They're doin' it for him.
Addy: For Iron Mike! Iron Mike! Iron Mike! Iron Mike!

[Just then, even more bikers come in from the northern highway.]

Rikki: Oh, and I hope you don't mind. I sent word to some of your friends up
       north.

Addy: Once word got around that we were fightin' back, we couldn't keep 'em
      away.

Deacon: Cope!

Copeland: Got word you were plannin' a little road trip. Stop these Militia
          sonsofbitches from comin' in here, tellin' us what to do. Since
          you've done so much for us, thought we'd come along.

Deacon: We'll be glad to have ya. Manny —
Manny: Heya¹ Deek —
Deacon: Nose down?

Manny: Nose down, work hard — they feed you. Take you on damn fool errands,
       get your ass shot off.

Deacon: Manny, listen up¹ this is a —
Manny: No way — no way I'm stayin' out of this.

[Even more bikers ride in.]

Deacon: Are you kiddin' me? The Hot Springs?

Rikki: Yep.

Addy: I sent word to Alkai.

Alkai: Deek.

Deacon: Hello¹ Alkai.

Alkai: Tucker sends word that¹ uh — she couldn't make it to the fight, but
       wishes she could be here.

Deacon: Yeah, I'll bet.

Alkai: That we wouldn't be here if it wasn't for your help. We're here to
       return the favor.

Deacon: Alright — okay. Well, you guys ready to kick some Militia ass?

[The Salome folks cheer.]

Alkai: We're ready to ride.

[Deek shakes his hand and goes in front of all the groups.]

Deacon: Alright, listen up! The plan is simple. Boozer and I are gonna hit the
        North Gate, we're gonna blow it to hell, and that's gonna pull everyone
        at the South Gate. And what you gotta do, is just follow Rikki. Yeah?
        Are we ready? How about you two, are we ready? Listen, I'm gonna radio
        when we hit the bridge. Don't go in until then.

Rikki: Okay.

Deacon: Alright! Let's do this!

[He climbs onto Boozer's armored dump truck.]

Deacon: For Iron Mike.

[Everyone gets into positions during the night. Boozer and Deacon race toward
 the North Gate.]

Deacon: Hey, Boozer, we gotta jump! Hey, Boozeman, time to go!

Boozer: We got one shot at this¹ brother!

Deacon: Dammit, Boozer.

Boozer: Go. Get your ol' lady.

[He leans out the window quickly and knocks Deacon off the truck and into the
 water alongside the North Gate's bridge.]

Deacon: Boozer!

[The North Gate blows up, sending the palisade flying like matchsticks.]

Deacon: No. No.

[He swims to Wizard Island and crawls into the mayhem.]

Deacon: Boozer — why didn't you jump — You shoulda — you shoulda jumped —
        Boozer — Oh Goddammit¹ Boozer — oh Goddammit —

[He emerges past the gate's wreckage.]

Deacon: I am going to kill — every Goddamn one of you! Sarah, Sarah — I gotta
        get to Sarah — A heavy — oh Goddammit — Oh¹ you're not gonna stop me —
        Hang on — Sarah! — I'm almost there — Ark — I gotta get to the ark —

[Just then, the ark's lower entrance explodes. He can hear Skizzo nearby.]

Skizzo: It's sealed! Come on, get to the upper cave. Move it! Go! Get up there
        and start setting charges. I said go, Goddammit! Go!

[When Deacon gets up, Skizzo's already gone.]

Deacon: Skizzo — sonofabitch Skizzo — I'm coming, Skizzo — Oh, well now we
        gotta do it the hard way — Top of the cone — gotta get to the top of
        the cone — I gotta find a way past these guys — Flamethrower — shit,
        shit, shit —

[Deek fights his way up the cone's winding exterior road.]

Deacon: Sniper — gotta be on the, uh — tower — Gotta take him out — gotta take
        him out — Gotta get past these guys — Almost there — Come on, come on —
        keep going —

[Down below, he can see fighting at the South Gate.]

Deacon: Rikki — can you hear me?
Rikki: Deek — we got 'em — we — we got 'em — Deek? Deek?
Deacon: Rikki? Rikki? Ah, give 'em hell¹ Rikki — burn 'em to the ground.

[Deek finally makes it to the summit.]

Deacon: Made it — finally — Hang on¹ Sarah — Sniper — get down —

[Deek hears soldiers planting charges in the cone's inner ramp system.]

Officer: Hurry it up already.
Soldier: Fuck you. You want me to blow us both to hell?
Officer: Goddammit, you hear that? Hurry up.
Soldier: There. It's good to go.
Officer: Alright. How many is that?
Soldier: Enough.
Officer: Let's get back to the Colonel. C'mon.

[Deek hears a convo on the radio.]

Officer: Captain Sarkozi, reporting in — we —
Skizzo: How many explosives did you set?
Officer: Captain, we didn't have time to set them all —
Skizzo: What? Goddammit — how many?
Officer: Uh — it — it's — it's — three. Three, sir.

Skizzo: Okay, okay. I'm going down to get the detonator from Weaver — you hold
        the cave entrance — you got that? No one gets down here.

Officer: Yes¹ sir, understood¹ sir. No one gets down.
Skizzo: And stay off this Goddamn channel — it might have been compromised —
Deacon: Skizzo — oh¹ you sonofabitch — Three explosives — I gotta find 'em —

[Deek descends into the cone, coming across a remote charge.]

Deacon: Here's one — I gotta disarm it — There — Okay, Goddammit — where's the
        others? I'm coming, Skizzo — wait for me —

[He finds another explosive.]

Deacon: Okay — okay — here's the second one — Come on¹ you sonofabitch —
        There — okay, that should do it. One more. Gotta find the last one —
        Almost there, Skizzo — almost there —

[Later, he finds another.]

Deacon: Here it is — Careful — careful — Got it — That's it — sorry, but you're
        not blowing up shit today, Skizzo — not today — Where ya hiding — huh?
        Nothing is going to stop me, Skizzo —

136) FOR AN OUTLAW BIKER                                                 [M136]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[In the nursery, Skizzo is threatening to slit Weaver's throat.]

Skizzo: Come on¹ Lieutenant. Where's that Goddamn detonator?
Weaver: Fuck you, man, I ain't getting trapped in here!

Skizzo: Weaver, come on, you know we follow orders. That's how it has to be.
        Where the fuck is it?! Weaver — where's the Goddamn detonator — give
        it to me —

Weaver: I don't know what you're talking about —
Skizzo: Don't make me kill you —
Weaver: You kill me — you ain't gettin' shit —
Skizzo: Weaver — Goddammit —
Weaver: Fuck you, Skizzo —
Deacon: Skizzo — you better let him go —

[If Deacon lollygags too long, Skizzo slits Weaver's throat.]

Deacon: Oh Goddammit —

[However, that's an automatic game over. Deek saves Weaver by firing on Skiz.]

Deacon: Yes! You sonofabitch —
Skizzo: Fuck!
Deacon: Hey! Hey.

[Skizzo runs off and leaves heavily armed lackeys in his place.]

Deacon: Weaver — get the hell outta here — go on, go! — I've got some people
        coming out of the North Gate — go!

[Weaver leaves the area. Skizzo continues to taunt Deacon.]

Skizzo: You are one stubborn sonofabitch — you know that?! I heard what you
        did¹ Deek — I heard what you did — killin' all those Rippers! Oh yeah,
        you drowned 'em like they was a buncha fuckin' rats! You did the world
        a solid — but I'll bet you that Iron Mike didn't see it that way, did
        he?! Yeah, I want you to know — that I — I didn't wanna kill that old
        man — I didn't — I didn't want to, Deek — huh? But he gave me no
        fuckin' choice — I tried to make him see reason — but he just fuckin'
        wouldn't — he just fuckin' wouldn't! You must wanna kill me real bad —
        huh? Huh? Follow me all the way back here — You came back here for her,
        huh? Didn't you? Oh yeah, you came back for your girl. Well, I got bad
        news for you, Deacon St. John — After Kouri broke you out, the Colonel
        didn't feel too happy about that — no¹ sir. He broke her like a fuckin'
        egg — he cracked her like an egg!

[He eliminates all of Skizzo's heavy infantry.]

Deacon: Skizzo! We end this — now!

[Deek pursues, but is caught in an explosion triggered by Skizzo.]

Deacon: Sonofabitch — I'm gonna kill you — with my bare hands — ya got that?

[Deek gets in closer as Skizzo fires in his direction.]

Skizzo: No — no! Damn you — die¹ Goddammit!

[He closes the distance and struggles with Skizzo. The bastard tries stabbing
 Deacon, but gets overpowered; the knife goes right into his abdomen.]

Deacon: You know something, Skizzo? There was a time when I would've¹ uh —
        Dragged you out into the shit —

Skizzo: No —

Deacon: And I woulda left you to the Freaks. But — hey, hey, hey, hey, hey.
        I'm not gonna do that. You wanna know why? Because they would tear you
        limb from limb — But you know what? They wouldn't enjoy it.

[He slits Skizzo's throat. In the distance, Garret's mad ravings echo.]

Garret: Shut up! All of you! I know what's happening out there — out there! —
        outside the ark! But it's — out — there. We are safe. In here. Nothing
        can touch us. Do you hear me? God has ordained this place — this is —
        consecrated ground. We are safe in this place. We are — safe — in this
        place.

[Deacon descends to Garret's private chambers. He's sitting at a table with
 Sarah and some bodyguards in attendance.]

Garret: I don't know — when or why¹ but — I — uh — I — I saw something. A — a
        month ago maybe. I — I felt something. Something I — I hadn't felt in
        a long time, and — um — And I know that a lot of you might have — might
        have felt the same way and I — I think that if we just — can —

Sarah: Deacon —
Garret: I'll have your side¹ arm.

[He has a gun on Sarah, so Deacon complies, throwing his gun to the side.]

Garret: Sit.
Deacon: Let' em go, Colonel. It's all over — your Militia is done.

Garret: Would you like some tea? I'm sure you would. Sarah, would you pour the
        Drifter a cup of tea.¹ The ark was our — our hope. You realize that, of
        course.

[As Garret drinks his tea, Sarah pours and shakes her head at Deacon.]

Garret: When the world was cleansed, it was the only thing that would allow us
        to rebuild. Everything was here, protected, saved by the grace of God.
        We never did find someone to play the piano though, did we? Ah, it
        doesn't matter now. When all this is gone, there'll be nobody left to
        hear the music. You've destroyed us. You destroyed everything we worked
        for.

Deacon: No¹ Colonel. You did. When you started this holy war. You know — given
        the choice between you and the Freaks — I'm gonna have to go with them.
        Because at least when they kill, they're just lookin' for a meal. And
        they don't kill unarmed women.

[He points a revolver at Deacon.]

Sarah: No!

[She struggles with the gun and gets whacked in the face for her effort. Deek
 struggles as well, but halfway through, the Colonel simply drops dead. He
 spills his teacup, revealing the hemlock inside the "herbal" brew.]

Sarah: You came back. Come on. Okay. Let's go.

[Outside, some of the fires rage, but the battle has ended. People are being
 treated and some are captured.]

Sarah: Oh my God. Hey, where's Boozer?
Deacon: He's gone.
Sarah: Oh shit. Why don't you go get some water, okay?
Deacon: Okay, okay.
Sarah: Hey, uh, could you set up a triage tent over there?

[Sarah walks off with a survivor; Deacon does the same with someone else.]

Deacon: Hey. Hey. There's a cave entrance over there. You'll find supplies and
        bandages. Get some men, go. Rikki! Addy!

Addy: I can help. I'm a doctor.

[Addy, responding to some cries for help, walks off.]

Rikki: It's over. Everyone that wasn't killed or wounded by the blast pretty
       much just gave up. Where's Boozer?

Addy: Rikki, I need some help over here! Rikki!
Rikki: Yeah. Um — What do you need help with?

[Rikki wanders off to Addy. Suddenly, from behind Deacon...]

Boozer: Hey. Hope you saved some for me.
Deacon: Boozer.
Boozer: Sorry I'm late.
Deacon: No —
Boozer: Yeah.
Deacon: No, no, no —
Boozer: I jumped.
Deacon: No — what the fuck — you were —
Boozer: Just before I ran outta bridge — yeah —
Deacon: I saw the truck —

Boozer: No, no, no, I felt the blast wave — Even under ten feet a' water. Now
        that was a ride!

Deacon: You did —

[They hug it out.]

Deacon: What —

Boozer: What? You didn't think I'd blow myself up¹ did ya? Then who'd be around
        to bust your balls?

Sarah: I would.
Boozer: Hey, hey. Oh — Little sister.
Sarah: Hey.

[She looks at his arm.]

Sarah: Oh —
Boozer: Yeah, yeah, long story. So, um — I hear someone's been lookin' for ya.
Deacon: Wha —
Boozer: Kinda wouldn't shut up about it.
Deacon: Yeah, don't listen to him. It was really — More his idea than it —
Boozer: Rikki! Addy! Which one a' you's drivin' me outta this shithole?

[Around dusk, everyone gathers at the top of the cone. Weaver hands him a flag
 removed from the flagpole.]

Weaver: It's all yours, brother.
Deacon: So, I hear that you're staying on to rebuild.
Weaver: Not all the Colonel's ideas were bad. Just the batshit crazy ones.
Deacon: You're the second person to tell me that.
Weaver: Who else? Kouri? You know what? Fuck that dude.
Deacon: Hey —
Weaver: He left us here to rot.
Deacon: If it wasn't for him we'd all be dead.

Weaver: Whatever, man. And I think we'll try this again without all the army
        man bullshit.

[Weaver starts leaving with his headphones in.]

Deacon: Hey. You're gonna miss my speech.
Weaver: Nah, I wouldn't say I'm gonna "miss" it.

[He walks over to some of the other community bigshots.]

Copeland: Deek. Helluva fight.
Deacon: Yeah, that it was. Manny. Ho, shit, look who's still breathin'.
Manny: Nose down.
Deacon: Nose down.
Manny: Keep it on your face that way.
Alkai: Not bad for a Drifter.

[Deek goes over to Boozer after.]

Deacon: Brother —
Boozer: We did it. You did it.

Deacon: Ah¹ man. You know I got to, uh — Admit for a second there I thought
        that you were, um —

Boozer: Gonna blow myself up? I told you, I got shit to do.
Deacon: Uh, well —
Boozer: Give 'em hell, brother.
Deacon: Yeah, here goes.
Boozer: Jack would be proud.

[Addy and Rikki are nearby.]

Addy: You did it.
Deacon: We did it. Come here.
Rikki: See? Good things happen when you stop and light a candle.
Deacon: Well¹ this is sort of more of a bonfire, but — yeah.
Rikki: Right —

[Deek walks over to his wife.]

Sarah: I've never seen you give a speech before.
Deacon: Oh, c'mon, it ain't gonna be a speech.
Sarah: Okay.
Deacon: Ma'am.

[She notices she's still wearing a Militia armband. She tosses it in the fire.]

Sarah: Shit. That's enough of that.
Deacon: Ah, what does it mean, that they're all getting quiet?
Sarah: Oh yeah. They're waiting for you. That's your cue.
Deacon: Goddammit. Sonofa —

[He addresses the crowd.]

Deacon: I know we got a lot of rebuilding to do, so I'm gonna keep this short.
        Look, I'm not a leader. I don't care what you say. I'm not. But, um.
        You've done something here today — we've done something. We banded
        together to fight. Not because some asshole told us to — But because
        it was the right thing to do. And you know what? We won! You know, I've
        seen you struggle. To rebuild. I've seen you fight to save lives. To
        keep people safe, keep people fed. I've seen you sacrifice everything
        that you have, everything that you are — To make the world a better
        place. And see — That's why we're still here. That's why we're still
        here. Because if we don't have hope, for a better life, or for a future
        that matters? The hell are we fighting for? You know, Iron Mike¹ he,
        um — He once said to me that — that we make the world what it is by
        what we do. Huh? What did we do? Huh? What are we going to do? You
        see this?

[He unfurls the Militia flag in his hands.]

Deacon: This is the first step.

[He tosses it on the fire.]

Sarah: I thought you weren't gonna give a speech.
Deacon: Yeah, I screwed up. Uh — how the hell was it?
Sarah: Oh, you know, it was — it was alright. For an outlaw biker.
Deacon: Outlaw biker, huh? Well, you ready to ride, old lady?
Sarah: I don't know, depends. Where are we going?
Deacon: Wherever the hell we want.

[They kiss in front of the bonfire. Roll credits as everyone travels back from
 Wizard Island to their respective communities.]

137) WHERE'S MY DAMN RINGS?                                              [M137]

[The first post-game mission has Deacon returning to Wizard Island to find the

Deacon: Here they are. Good.

[He picks up Sarah's wedding ring.]

Deacon: I do, sweetheart.

138) FOR THE BENEFIT OF OTHERS                                           [M138]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[Later, Deek meets Rikki and Addy at the Lost Lake cemetery.]

Deacon: Hey.
Addy: Hey¹ Deacon.

[He looks at Iron Mike's grave marker.]

Rikki: Addy carved it herself. It's beautiful, right?

Addy: Thanks. Yeah, it was a piece of redwood Mike kept in his room. He once
      told me that when things settled down, he was going to make something
      out of it, like a — cribbage board.

Deacon: Wait, a what? A — he doesn't — play cribbage. Iron Mike played
        cribbage?

Addy: No. No, but that's the point. That there'd come a day when something like
      that mattered again.

Deacon: Well, what does it say?
Addy: Don't look at me,¹ I just carved it.

Rikki: It's, uh — it's an old Hindu proverb. My mother taught it to me. It
       reads — "Rivers do not drink their own water. Trees do not eat their
       own fruit. And clouds do not swallow their own rain. What great ones
       have is always for the benefit of others." What do you think?

Addy: Well, coming from you, I think that would have meant a lot to him.

Deacon: Yeah. Yeah, I think if Mike were here he would probably say something
        like —  "What — the hell does that even mean?" Huh? C'mon.

[They have a good laugh.]

Rikki: Yeah — no, you're right. He woulda said, "What the hell does that mean?"

Deacon: Followed by "What the hell are you doin' standin' around here? The
        world ain't gonna save itself Goddammit. Get to work."

Rikki: Yep. You're right again. C'mon¹ guys, let's get to work.

[They start walking away.]

Rikki: Oh, did I ever tell you about the time Iron Mike — Saw Addy and I for
       the first time at the lodge in front of the fireplace¹ —

Addy: Oh, this is funny.
Rikki: Okay, so we were tangled up —
Addy: No, no, no, no — we were all up in it —
Rikki: Okay, Addy — Addy —
Deacon: What — uh — uh — why
Rikki: For the first time, and Iron Mike comes out. And he looks at us —
Deacon: You don't have to tell me this. You can stop.
Rikki: He had that grin on his face.
Deacon: I'm not grin —
Rikki: You're such a perv, Deek!
Deacon: Oh my God. I'm tired a' you two.
Addy: You are a perv.

_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
139) I'M NOT A RIPPER                                                    [M139]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[At some point, Deacon walks near the Lost Lake main gate and finds Lisa being
 held at gunpoint.]

Guard: Hey! We got a Goddamn Ripper here! Turn around!
Lisa: I'm not a Ripper!

Deacon: Hey! Whoa, whoa, whoa, hold up, hold up, hold up. I know her. Uh — put
        that away, I got this.

Guard: Okay. Take care of her. Not my problem.

[He leaves Deacon and Lisa in awkward silence.]

Deacon: Is — is this your ride?
Lisa: It's a piece of shit — but it runs.

Deacon: Uh, well, I don't know if you're stickin' around but I could have Rikki
        take a look at it.

Lisa: I brought some bounties. To trade.

[He looks in her bloody bag of severed ears.]

Deacon: Okay. Then, uh, I should probably introduce you to — Joe Haslin, he's
        the bounty collector. He's right up this way.

Lisa: I'm not staying. I'm not staying in a Goddamn camp.

Deacon: Yeah, do whatever you want. You know, while you're here, uh, I'd like
        to introduce you, uh — To someone. Her name is Sarah. She had a kid
        sister that¹ um — Well, her kid sister reminds me of you. So I thought
        that maybe you — would like her.

Lisa: I had a sister. She was older than me. A pain in my ass.

Deacon: Kinda reminds me of my older brother, Boozer, a real pain in the ass —
        Actually he — he's not my brother, um — We rode together in the M.C.
        And he's the head of security around here, so you should probably meet
        him too.

Lisa: I told you I'm not staying.

Deacon: And I heard you. Seriously, do whatever you want. So what kinda gun
        you got there? Are you making sure that you ride out with plenty of
        ammo?

Lisa: Yeah, I got enough, I'm good.
Deacon: Oh, I always rather had to work at that.

[They walk through the front gate together.]

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
140) THERE'S NOTHING YOU CAN DO                                          [M140]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[While exploring the world, Deacon suddenly gets a call.

O'Brian: St. John. Are you there?
Deacon: O'Brian? Wha — why are you on this channel?
O'Brian: We tried — contacting you on our channel —
Deacon: Well, I lost the radio the night that shit went down.
O'Brian: Did she make it out? Your wife?
Deacon: Yeah, no thanks to you.
O'Brian: I'm glad. There's — something that I have to tell you.
Deacon: So talk.
O'Brian: In person.
Deacon: Nah, I don't think so.
O'Brian: It's important.
Deacon: Shit.
O'Brian: In the Northern Cascades, there's an old pioneer cemetery —
Deacon: Yeah¹ okay — I know the one.
O'Brian: Meet me there. Please.

[Deek goes out to the cemetery, as requested. A helo is parked in the lot
 where Alvarez died early in the game.]

Deacon: Well, I can't say I expected to hear from you again. What is it this
        time?

O'Brian: Believe it or not, I'm glad to see you again. That night at Wizard
         Island didn't seem to go well.

Deacon: What can I do for you, O'Brian?

O'Brian: I'm here to warn you.

Deacon: Warn me? Warn me about what?

O'Brian: You remember, I told you the freaks are evolving.¹

Deacon: Right, yeah, a Freak's a Freak. What the hell do I care?

[O'Brian takes off his helmet, revealing a bald, eerily pale head, almost like
 an silent film nosferatu. His voice modulation doesn't work properly.]

O'Brian: The strain of the virus, its effects on the human nervous and
         lymphatic systems — is accelerating at an exponential rate. They knew
         all along, of course. That it was happening — The men above me? That's
         why they were so cautious. So secretive. They're coming. I'm sorry.
         There's nothing you can do to stop them. There's nothing anyone can
         do.

[As the helicoper starts taking off, O'Brian jumps vertically and quickly
 catches on, then pulls himself in at inhuman speed.]

Deacon: What the fuck?

[The helo disappears in the distance. After, Copeland has a timely message.]

Copeland: This is Radio Free Oregon. The Truth Shall Set You Free. You heard
          me talking about the black choppers, NERO choppers. Well, none have
          been sighted in days. But don't cool your heels just yet. NERO isn't
          done, not by a long shot. With NERO out of the skies, that can only
          mean one thing: they got what they're after and they've all flown
          back to their coops. This is the end game, friends. The Feds have
          had this plan ready long before the Freaks. Now they're gonna roll
          over the earth, and woe to anyone who stands in their way. But we've
          hung on this long; we're not gonna give up now. We're fighters. We've
          survived two years in the shit. In the Freakshow. And we are nothing
          if not prepared.

Deacon: Like I said before — Cope — you don't know the half of it. But yeah,
        yeah, I'm with ya on this one — it ain't over yet.

A BUNCH OF CAVEMEN                                                       [SD01]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After "I Don't Wanna Hang," Deek visits Kouri at Diamond Lake.]

Kouri: Deacon. Good. I've got an important mission for you.
Deacon: That's why I'm here — sir.

Kouri: A group of Marauders has been attacking supply lines on our southern
       border. I've marked their position on your map. We think they're using
       a network of caves, south of Crater Lake, as their base of operations.

Deacon: Caves — okay.
Kouri: I don't have enough resources available for a full-on assault —
Deacon: So you want me to go in — quiet — and take 'em out.
Kouri: I'll leave the details up to you, Corporal. Dismissed.

[He goes out to the camp.]

Deacon: Captain — I found the Marauders who've been harassing our supply lines.
        Just where you said they'd be.

Kouri: Corporal St. John — good. Do you need assistance?

Deacon: Ah, they look pretty ragtag — I think I got this.

Kouri: Good luck, Corporal. Kouri out.

[Deek infiltrates the ridge base.]

Deacon: So you boys thought you'd just set up camp — pick off Militia supply
        runs, is that it? Ya gotta know life's not that easy.

[Soon, the seven marauders are slain.]

Deacon: Is that all of 'em? Okay, yeah. They're done. Corporal St. John to
        Diamond Lake. Come in.

Kouri: Corporal.

Deacon: Captain. Those Marauders on our southern border — have been — uh —
        neutralized.

Kouri: You said "our."
Deacon: Sir?

Kouri: You were a Drifter for a long time, St. John. Sometimes it takes a
       while for — a new recruit to accept their position as part of a greater
       force. Frankly, I didn't know if you could do it.

Deacon: Uh, well, hey — I'm in the army now —
Kouri: Yes — yes¹ you are. Dismissed¹ Corporal.
Deacon: Uh, yes¹ sir. St. John out.

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
A HELL OF A FIGHT                                                        [SD02]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After "You Alone I Have Seen," Deek returns to Diamond Lake for a mission.]

Kouri: Corporal St. John. I've got an urgent assignment for you.

Deacon: Sorta assumed that's why you radioed me to report in — sir.

Kouri: One of our patrols has been wiped out. I sent another patrol to find
       them and all of our men have been accounted for but one.

Deacon: Private Gomez? Yeah — is she alive?

Kouri: I don't know. Tracks from the site lead in all directions. I need
       someone with your — unique skills to go to the site and check it out.

Deacon: Okay. I'll do what I can.

Kouri: I know I can count on you, St. John. Dismissed.

[Deacon goes to Gomez's last-known location.]

Deacon: Okay — let's take a look around. Militia bike — Gomez — that's gotta
        be hers. Okay, tracks — female-sized boots — that could be hers. More
        blood — oh, God — I hope it's not all hers. Bloody bootprint — yeah,
        that's gotta be hers.

[He follows the tracks to a marauder fort, then kills them all.]

Deacon: Okay. That's it — they're all dead.

[Deek ascends the fire tower.]

Deacon: Gomez — you in here?

Gomez: Hey, hey, hey, hey — I'm in here! St. John, hey! I'm in here — c'mon,
       buddy, I'm in here! St. John — I'm in here, where are you?

Deacon: Hold on. Gomez. Good to see ya breathing.
Gomez: St. John. Never thought I'd be glad to see your ugly mug.

Deacon: Hey, you got any blood left in that scrawny ass a' yours? It looks like
        you were tryin' to leave it all over the campus.

Gomez: It wasn't all mine.

Deacon: Okay. Are you good to go? Because your bike's still out front,¹ looks
        like a piece of shit — but I think it's probably that way before, you
        know?

Gomez: I could still beat your ass in a fair race.
Deacon: Yeah, yeah.
Gomez: Hey, St. John? Thanks.
Deacon: Go on, get outta here.

[Deek mounts up after Gomez leaves.]

Deacon: Corporal St. John to Captain Kouri. I, uh — found her, sir. Private
        Gomez is on her way back.

Kouri: St. John. Good work.

Deacon: I'll radio in to check on her. St. John out.

[Later...]

Deacon: St. John to Kouri. Captain, just, uh — checkin' in to make sure Gomez
        made it back okay.

Kouri: Yes. Private Gomez was very grateful. She said that if it weren't for
       you, she would have been killed.

Deacon: Uh — just doing my job, Captain. St¹ John out.
