WE DO NOT DISCRIMINATE                                                   [SD40]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After "I Know Things Are Strange," Deacon gets a call.]

Kouri: St. John. This is Captain Kouri. Come in.
Deacon: Yeah, Captain. I'm here.

Kouri: Well I just wanted to let you know that the Colonel gives an informal —
       talk — every day at dusk. At the staging area where you were sworn in,

Deacon: Uh — yes¹ sir.

Kouri: Now, while these talks are "informal," enlisted men and women are
       expected to attend.

Deacon: Uh — copy that. Sir.
Kouri: Kouri out.
Deacon: Oh, great. A commander who likes to give fireside chats. Can't wait.

[Deek goes to the staging grounds for his first speech.]

Garret: These past few days, dozens of new recruits have joined our ranks. We
        welcome you. We do not care about the color of your skin. We do not
        care what country you were born in. We do not care if you are a man or
        a woman. We do not care if you are gay or lesbian or bisexual or
        transgender. These are things — beyond your control. These are things
        that God has ordained. And we accept them. What we do not accept are
        liars, thieves, rapists, murderers, fornicators, adulterers, oath
        breakers, drug addicts, or criminals of any kind — From this life or
        the one before. How you conduct yourself, how you act in the eyes of
        God — these are things that you do control. Any soldier, or officer,
        found guilty of any transgression — no matter how small — Will be
        brought here, to this very scaffold, and will be hanged by the neck
        until they are dead. This punishment may seem cruel to some of you.
        But you have my promise — any punishment of ours is a great mercy
        compared to the punishment of God that is being unleashed on the world
        outside these walls. None of us is perfect. We do not expect
        perfection. What we do expect — is obedience, order and discipline.
        Give us these things, and we will win this war. Company dismissed.

WE MUST FILL THE ARK                                                     [SD41]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After "Afraid of a Little Competition?," Deacon attends another speech.]

Garret: Many of you have been with me from the beginning. Listened to me when
        I warned about the coming of God's plague. Journeyed with me to this
        place. Helped me to build this ark. But whether you were with us from
        the beginning, or joined our ranks only today — You — are now part of
        this great endeavor. You — are now part of our mission to save mankind.
        I want to remind you, as you go forth beyond these walls to perform
        your duties, that we are still searching for material worthy — Of
        safekeeping within the ark. We seek textbooks, manuals, encyclopediae,
        discs, and other media. Lieutenant Weaver has listed several books on
        chemistry that are needed. Lieutenant Whitaker has listed books on
        biochemistry, genetics, and biology that we are lacking. Captain
        Jiminez has listed books on medicine, anatomy, and surgical procedures that we need. Sergeant Tomlinson — has listed books on highway
        construction, mechanical engineering. And Captain Hawkins is always
        looking for material related to agriculture and hydroponics. So — while
        you're out doing runs, keep an eye out for items like these. Do your
        part — to help us fill the ark. Company dismissed.

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
YOU DON'T WANT TO KNOW                                                   [SD42]
_______________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

[After the talk in "How Far We Have Fallen," Deek sets out to find Meyers.]

Deacon: Okay, Private Meyers — where the hell are you?

[Deek slays two bikers nearby.]

Deacon: Wait a second, are those the men that you were riding with? Oh, Jesus —

[He follows up the road.]

Deacon: Where the hell are you, Meyers —

[An frosty foe-filled encampment is nearby.]

Deacon: Anarchists — okay, I gotta be careful — gotta be careful.

[After slaying more bikers, Deacon climbs into the camp.]

Deacon: This is it —

[He follows a trail to a corpse -- Meyers, who was tortured and stabbed.]

Deacon: Oh, yeah — that's him. Oh, yeah — here it is. Okay, Meyers, uh — I
        would tell ya — Rest in Peace — but — oh boy, you don't want any of
        that. Okay, good — just gotta get this back to the Colonel.

[Back at Wizard Island...]

Deacon: Colonel Garret — sir?
Garret: Corporal — St. John, is it?

Deacon: Yes¹ sir. I, uh — I tracked down that AWOL soldier — Private Meyers.
        And — here is your Bible.

Garret: And God Almighty shall have the final word. Did you bring him back
        alive? We have a noose waiting for him in the staging area.

Deacon: Uh — no, sir. Um — the Anarchists got to him before I did. And they
        tortured him to death.

Garret: Unfortunate. But God's will is God's justice.
Deacon: Uh — yes¹ sir.
Garret: Carry on, Corporal.
